add_namespace = israel_news

add_namespace = israel_mechanic #Events for the mechanics + historical stuff
add_namespace = israel.coalition

country_event = {
	id = israel.coalition.0
	title = israel.coalition.0.t
	desc = israel.coalition.0.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_israeli_government_event
	option = {
		name = israel.coalition.0.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: israel.coalition.0.a"
		set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.05 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		add_political_power = 200
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = israel.coalition.1
	title = israel.coalition.1.t
	desc = israel.coalition.1.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_liberman_event
	option = {
		name = israel.coalition.1.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: israel.coalition.1.a"
		add_stability = -0.07
		set_temp_variable = {
			party_index = 15
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			party_popularity_increase = 0.03
		}
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { remove_col_one = 15 }
			remove_coalition_members_effect = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = ISR_liberman_left_TT
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = israel.coalition.11
	title = israel.coalition.11.t
	desc = israel.coalition.11.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_israeli_government_event
	option = {
		name = israel.coalition.11.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: israel.coalition.11.a"
		if = {
			limit = {
				40_percent_government_popularity = yes
				NOT = {
					60_percent_government_popularity = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = ISR_big_size_knesset }
				clr_country_flag = ISR_big_size_knesset
				set_country_flag = ISR_good_size_knesset
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = ISR_small_knesset }
				clr_country_flag = ISR_small_knesset
				set_country_flag = ISR_good_size_knesset
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				60_percent_government_popularity = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = ISR_good_size_knesset }
				clr_country_flag = ISR_good_size_knesset
				set_country_flag = ISR_big_size_knesset
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = ISR_small_knesset }
				clr_country_flag = ISR_small_knesset
				set_country_flag = ISR_big_size_knesset
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = arab_completed }
			clear_variable = arab_completed
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = meretz_completed }
			clear_variable = meretz_completed
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = labour_completed }
			clear_variable = labour_completed
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = jewish_completed }
			clear_variable = jewish_completed
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = nz_completed }
			clear_variable = nz_completed
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = jud_completed }
			clear_variable = jud_completed
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = shas_completed }
			clear_variable = shas_completed
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = likud_completed }
			clear_variable = likud_completed
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = givir_completed }
			clear_variable = givir_completed
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = liberam_completed }
			clear_variable = liberam_completed
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = israel.coalition.12
	title = israel.coalition.12.t
	desc = israel.coalition.12.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_israeli_government_event
	option = {
		name = israel.coalition.12.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: israel.coalition.12.a"
		if = {
			limit = {
				10_percent_government_popularity = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = ISR_good_size_knesset }
				clr_country_flag = ISR_good_size_knesset
				set_country_flag = ISR_small_knesset
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = ISR_big_size_knesset }
				clr_country_flag = ISR_big_size_knesset
				set_country_flag = ISR_small_knesset
			}
			country_event = {
				id = MD4_election_campaign.0
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = israel.coalition.13
	title = israel.coalition.13.t
	desc = israel.coalition.13.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		check_variable = {
			government_collapse = 2
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_israeli_government_event
	option = {
		name = israel.coalition.13.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: israel.coalition.13.a"
		set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.2 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = -0.05 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = ISR_good_size_knesset }
			clr_country_flag = ISR_good_size_knesset
			set_country_flag = ISR_small_knesset
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = ISR_big_size_knesset }
			clr_country_flag = ISR_big_size_knesset
			set_country_flag = ISR_small_knesset
		}
		country_event = {
			id = MD4_election_campaign.0
		}
		clear_variable = government_collapse
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = israel.knesset.0
	title = israel.knesset.0.t
	desc = israel.knesset.0.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_israeli_government_event
	option = {
		name = israel.knesset.0.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: israel.knesset.0.a"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = ISR_good_size_knesset
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = bill_support
				value = 50
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = ISR_big_size_knesset
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = bill_support
				value = 70
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = ISR_big_size_knesset
				has_idea = ISR_yesman_likud
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = bill_support
				value = 75
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = ISR_good_size_knesset
				has_idea = ISR_yesman_likud
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = bill_support
				value = 55
			}
		}
	}
}

					}

			}
		}
	}

##########warbetween_wars

###Kill sci of iran to show to ISR / big infl / SUCC
country_event = {
	id = israel_mechanic.9
	title = israel_mechanic.9.t
	desc = israel_mechanic.9.d
	picture = GFX_rocket_strike_isr_one
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = israel_mechanic.9.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: israel_mechanic.9.a executed"
		effect_tooltip = {
			PER = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = ISR_kill_scientist_idea
					days = 365
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = israel_mechanic.101
	title = israel_mechanic.101.t
	desc = israel_mechanic.101.d
	picture = GFX_rocket_strike_isr_two
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = israel_mechanic.101.a
		add_war_support = -0.05
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: israel_mechanic.101.a executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}
}

				add_timed_idea = {

					days = 365
				}
			}
		}

		}
	}
}

#############succ olympic games
country_event = {
	id = israel_mechanic.15
	title = israel_mechanic.15.t
	desc = israel_mechanic.15.d
	picture = GFX_retaliatory_strike
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = israel_mechanic.15.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: israel_mechanic.15.a executed"
		effect_tooltip = {
			ISR = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = ISR_olympic_games_op
					days = 365
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_dlc = "La Resistance"
					}
					add_intel = {
						target = PER
						civilian_intel = 15
						army_intel = 15
					}
					add_decryption = {
						target = PER
						ratio = 0.5
					}
				}
			}
			PER = {
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					damage_building = {
						type = nuclear_reactor
						damage = 1
					}
				}
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					damage_building = {
						type = nuclear_reactor
						damage = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}
}

#############fail olympic games
country_event = {
	id = israel_mechanic.16
	title = israel_mechanic.16.t
	desc = israel_mechanic.16.d
	picture = GFX_retaliatory_strike
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = israel_mechanic.16.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: israel_mechanic.13.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = ISR
			}
			add_war_support = -0.05
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = USA
			}
			add_war_support = -0.05
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = PER
			}
			add_war_support = 0.05
			add_stability = 0.05
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}
}

#############funny little event chain to steal nuclear archive
country_event = {
	id = israel_mechanic.17
	title = israel_mechanic.17.t
	desc = israel_mechanic.17.d
	picture = GFX_special_forces
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = israel_mechanic.17.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: israel_mechanic.13.a executed"
		set_temp_variable = {
			treasury_change = -6
		}
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		random_list = {
			40 = {
				country_event = israel_mechanic.18
			}
			60 = {
				country_event = israel_mechanic.19
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 2
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = israel_mechanic.17.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: israel_mechanic.13.b executed"
		add_political_power = -60
		hidden_effect = {
			PER = {
				country_event = israel_mechanic.1711
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			30 = {
				country_event = israel_mechanic.18
			}
			30 = {
				country_event = israel_mechanic.20
			}
			60 = {
				country_event = israel_mechanic.19
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = israel_mechanic.22
	title = israel_mechanic.22.t
	desc = israel_mechanic.22.d
	picture = GFX_rocket_strike_isr_two
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = israel_mechanic.22.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: israel_mechanic.22.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = ISR
			}
			add_political_power = 100
			army_experience = 10
			add_command_power = 10
			add_war_support = 0.05
			set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
			set_temp_variable = {
				party_popularity_increase = 0.05
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				temp_outlook_increase = 0.05
			}
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = PER
			}
			add_political_power = -100
			add_war_support = -0.05
			set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
			set_temp_variable = {
				party_popularity_increase = -0.05
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				temp_outlook_increase = -0.05
			}
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			set_temp_variable = {
				percent_change = -2
			}
			change_domestic_influence_percentage = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = HAM
			}
			add_political_power = -100
			add_war_support = -0.05
			set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
			set_temp_variable = {
				party_popularity_increase = -0.05
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				temp_outlook_increase = -0.05
			}
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			set_temp_variable = {
				percent_change = -3
			}
			change_domestic_influence_percentage = yes
			recalculate_party = yes
			update_government_coalition_strength = yes
			update_party_name = yes
			set_coalition_drift = yes
			set_ruling_leader = yes
			set_leader = yes
			retire_country_leader = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}
}

# ISR_fill_our_stocks, ISR_gather_all_the_equipment

country_event = {
	id = israel_economy.4
	title = israel_economy.4.t
	desc = israel_economy.4.d
	picture = GFX_israel_china
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = israel_economy.4.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: israel_economy.4.a executed"
		ISR = {
			country_event = israel_economy.5
		}
		newline = yes
		ISR = {
			set_temp_variable = {
				treasury_change = 10
			}
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
			if = {
				limit = { has_dlc = "By Blood Alone" }
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = small_plane_suicide_airframe_2
					amount = -50
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = Air_UAV1
					amount = -50
				}
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = command_control_equipment3
				amount = -250
			}
		}
		newline = yes
		CHI = {
			set_temp_variable = {
				treasury_change = -10
			}
			modify_treasury_effect = yes

				limit = { has_dlc = "By Blood Alone" }
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {

					amount = 50
					producer = ISR
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = Air_UAV1
					amount = 50
					producer = ISR
				}
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = command_control_equipment3
				amount = 250
				producer = ISR
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				sender_influence_higher_5 = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				sender_influence_higher_15 = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value > 15
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value > 50
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value > 100
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = israel_economy.4.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: israel_economy.4.b executed"
		ISR = {
			country_event = israel_economy.6
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = { # very high influence ensures acceptance
				factor = 0
				sender_influence_higher_30 = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value < -15
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value < -50

			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50

			}

# ISR_taba_conference
country_event = {
	id = israel_economy.119
	title = israel_economy.119.t
	desc = israel_economy.119.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_handshake_black
	option = {
		name = israel_economy.119.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: israel_economy.119.a executed"
		add_political_power = 50
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = ISR
			relation = non_aggression_pact
			active = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = econ_isr_boycotte
					has_idea = pol_isr_boycotte
				}
			}
			remove_ideas = econ_isr_boycotte
			remove_ideas = pol_isr_boycotte
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = full_isr_boycotte
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = full_isr_boycotte
				add_idea = econ_isr_boycotte
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			percent_change = 3
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			tag_index = EGY
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			influence_target = ISR
		}
		change_influence_percentage = yes
		ISR = {
			country_event = israel_economy.120
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				sender_influence_higher_5 = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				sender_influence_higher_15 = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				has_opinion = {

					value > 15
				}

		}

			percent_change = 2
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			tag_index = EGY
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			influence_target = PAL
		}
		change_influence_percentage = yes
		set_temp_variable = {
			percent_change = 5
		}
		change_domestic_influence_percentage = yes
		ISR = {
			country_event = israel_economy.121
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10

				party_popularity_increase = 0.05
			}
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}
}

# ISR_cento_iran
country_event = {
	id = israel_economy.125
	title = israel_economy.125.t
	desc = israel_economy.125.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_message_signing
	option = {
		name = israel_economy.125.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: israel_economy.125.a"
		ISR = {
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		add_to_faction = ISR
		ISR = {
			country_event = israel_economy.126
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				sender_influence_higher_5 = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				sender_influence_higher_15 = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value > 15
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value > 50
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value > 100
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = israel_economy.125.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: israel_economy.125.b"
		ISR = {
			country_event = israel_economy.127
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = { # very high influence ensures acceptance
				factor = 0
				sender_influence_higher_30 = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value < -15
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value < -50
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value < -100
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# ISR_enemy_of_my_enemy
country_event = {
	id = israel_economy.128
	title = israel_economy.128.t
	desc = israel_economy.128.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_CAN_tweet_saudi_outrage
	option = {
		name = israel_economy.128.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: israel_economy.128.a"
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = ISR
			relation = non_aggression_pact
			active = yes
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = full_isr_boycotte
			add_idea = econ_isr_boycotte
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = ISR
			modifier = has_expressed_loyalty
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = ISR
			modifier = has_expressed_loyalty
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			percent_change = 5
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			tag_index = ISR
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			influence_target = ROOT
		}
		change_influence_percentage = yes
		ISR = {
			country_event = israel_economy.129
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				sender_influence_higher_5 = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				sender_influence_higher_15 = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value > 15
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value > 50
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value > 100
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = israel_economy.128.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: israel_economy.128.b"
		ISR = {
			add_war_support = -0.05
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			modifier = diplomatic_disloyalty
			target = ISR
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			modifier = diplomatic_disloyalty
			target = ISR
		}
		ISR = {
			country_event = israel_economy.130
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = { # very high influence ensures acceptance
				factor = 0
				sender_influence_higher_30 = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value < -15
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value < -50
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value < -100
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# ISR_apologize_past_actions
country_event = {
	id = israel_economy.131
	title = israel_economy.131.t
	desc = israel_economy.131.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_handshake_black
	option = {
		name = israel_economy.131.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: israel_economy.131.a"
		set_temp_variable = {
			treasury_change = 2
		}
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = ISR
			modifier = tensions_eased
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = ISR
			modifier = tensions_eased
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			percent_change = 5
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			tag_index = ISR
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			influence_target = ROOT
		}
		change_influence_percentage = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = econ_isr_boycotte
					has_idea = pol_isr_boycotte
				}
			}
			remove_ideas = econ_isr_boycotte
			remove_ideas = pol_isr_boycotte
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = full_isr_boycotte
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = full_isr_boycotte
				add_idea = econ_isr_boycotte
			}
		}
		ISR = {
			country_event = israel_economy.132
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				sender_influence_higher_5 = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				sender_influence_higher_15 = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value > 15
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value > 50
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value > 100
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = israel_economy.131.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: israel_economy.131.b"
		ISR = {
			add_war_support = -0.05
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			modifier = diplomatic_disloyalty
			target = ISR
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			modifier = diplomatic_disloyalty
			target = ISR
		}
		ISR = {
			country_event = israel_economy.133
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = { # very high influence ensures acceptance
				factor = 0
				sender_influence_higher_30 = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value < -15
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value < -50
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value < -100
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# ISR_visit_oman
country_event = {
	id = israel_economy.134
	title = israel_economy.134.t
	desc = israel_economy.134.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_pdl_convention
	option = {
		name = israel_economy.134.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: israel_economy.134.a"
		OMA = {
			give_military_access = ISR
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = ISR
			modifier = diplomatic_support
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = ISR
			modifier = diplomatic_support
		}
		remove_ideas = econ_isr_boycotte
		set_temp_variable = {
			percent_change = 2
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			tag_index = ISR
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			influence_target = OMA
		}
		change_influence_percentage = yes
		ISR = {
			country_event = israel_economy.135
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				sender_influence_higher_5 = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				sender_influence_higher_15 = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value > 15
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value > 50
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value > 100
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {

		set_temp_variable = {
			percent_change = 5
		}
		change_domestic_influence_percentage = yes

			modifier = diplomatic_disloyalty

			target = ISR
		}

		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10

				factor = 0
				sender_influence_higher_30 = yes
			}

					target = ISR
					value < -15
				}

			modifier = {
				add = 30

					target = ISR
					value < -50

			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50

					value < -100

# ISR_exhibitions_dubai
country_event = {
	id = israel_economy.140
	title = israel_economy.140.t
	desc = israel_economy.140.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_message_signing
	option = {
		name = israel_economy.140.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: israel_economy.140.a"
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = ISR
			modifier = major_improve_trade
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = ISR
			modifier = major_improve_trade
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = econ_isr_boycotte
					has_idea = pol_isr_boycotte
				}
			}
			remove_ideas = econ_isr_boycotte
			remove_ideas = pol_isr_boycotte
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = full_isr_boycotte
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = full_isr_boycotte
				add_idea = econ_isr_boycotte
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			receiver_nation = ISR.id
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			sender_nation = UAE.id
		}
		set_improved_trade_agreement = yes
		ISR = {
			country_event = israel_economy.141
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				sender_influence_higher_5 = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				sender_influence_higher_15 = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value > 15
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value > 50
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value > 100
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = israel_economy.140.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: israel_economy.140.b"
		set_temp_variable = {
			percent_change = 2
		}
		change_domestic_influence_percentage = yes
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			modifier = diplomatic_disloyalty
			target = ISR
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			modifier = diplomatic_disloyalty
			target = ISR
		}
		ISR = {
			country_event = israel_economy.142
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = { # very high influence ensures acceptance
				factor = 0
				sender_influence_higher_30 = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value < -15
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value < -50
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value < -100
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				type = small_plane_strike_airframe_1

			}
		}
		else = {
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {

				amount = 55
				producer = GER
			}
		}

		}

# ISR_thyssenkrupp_deal
# AI always accepts
country_event = {
	id = israel.13
	title = israel.13.t
	desc = israel.13.d
	picture = GFX_internal_faction_religion
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = israel.13.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: israel.13.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = GER
			}
			set_country_flag = ThyssenKrupp_Corruption
			custom_effect_tooltip = ISR_GER_agree_to_sell_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
					}
					ISR = {
						set_technology = {
							attack_submarine_hull_1 = 1
						}
						load_oob = "ISR_buy_german_subs_MTG"
					}
				}
				else = {
					ISR = {
						set_technology = {
							diesel_attack_submarine_2 = 1
						}
						load_oob = "ISR_buy_german_subs"
					}
				}
				GER = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						treasury_change = 6
					}
					modify_treasury_effect = yes
				}
				ISR = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						treasury_change = -6
					}
					modify_treasury_effect = yes
					country_event = israel.14
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = israel.13.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: israel.13.b executed"
		ISR = {
			country_event = israel.15
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

# ISR_world_populists
country_event = {
	id = israel_likud.22
	title = israel_likud.22.t
	desc = israel_likud.22.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_israeli_government_event
	option = {
		name = israel_likud.22.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: israel_likud.22.a"
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 21 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.02 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.03 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		every_country = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_european_nation = yes
					NOT = {
						tag = POL
						tag = HUN
					}
				}
				country_event = israel_likud.23
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { tag = POL }
				country_event = israel_likud.24
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { tag = HUN }
				country_event = israel_likud.25
			}
		}
		USA = {
			country_event = israel_likud.26
		}
		BRA = {
			country_event = israel_likud.27
		}
	}
}

	option = { # only political support
		name = israel_likud.33.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: israel_likud.33.a"
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = ISR
			modifier = improve_relation
		}
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 3 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_index = USA }
		set_temp_variable = { influence_target = ISR }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
		ISR = {
			country_event = israel_likud.34
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value > 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # economic support
		name = israel_likud.33.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: israel_likud.33.b"
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = ISR modifier = has_expressed_loyalty }

			random_owned_state = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex

				}
			}
			country_event = israel_likud.35
		}
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -7.5 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				sender_influence_higher_5 = yes

					value > 5

				has_opinion = {

				}
			}

				add = 10

					target = ISR
					value > 100
				}
			}
		}

			}
		}

		change_influence_percentage = yes
		ISR = {
			country_event = israel_likud.36
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				sender_influence_higher_5 = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				sender_influence_higher_15 = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value > 15
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				has_opinion = {
					target = ISR
					value > 50
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10

					target = ISR
					value > 100
				}
			}

				factor = 3
